      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(document).ready(function () {
        var $scopeWrapper = $("#scope_selector_wrapper");

        $(".scope_selector_item", $scopeWrapper).on("mouseover", function () {
            var $parentElement = $(this).parent();
            var parentElement = $parentElement[0];
            if ($parentElement.hasClass("scope_level")) {
                $(".scope_has_child", $scopeWrapper).each(function (index, element) {
                    if (parentElement === element) {
                        $parentElement.toggleClass("scope_open");
                    } else {
                        $(element).removeClass("scope_open");
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        var $scopeSelBtnlabel = $('#scope_selector_btn_label');
        $(".scope_selector_item", $scopeWrapper).on("click", function () {
            $scopeSelBtnlabel.html($(this).text());
            $(".scope_open", $scopeWrapper).removeClass("scope_open");
            $scopeWrapper.removeClass("wrapper_open");
            $("#scopeSelector").val($(this).attr("data-code"));
            $(".scope_selector_selected", $scopeWrapper).removeClass("scope_selector_selected");
            $(this).addClass("scope_selector_selected");
        });
        var updateScopeSelectorPosition = function () {
            var offset = $("#scope_selector_btn").offset();
            var homeGridOffset = $('.home-grid').offset();
            $scopeWrapper.css({
                top: offset.top + 30 - $(window).scrollTop(),
                left: homeGridOffset.left - $(window).scrollLeft()
            });
        }
        $("#scope_selector_btn").on("click", function () {
            if ($scopeWrapper.hasClass("wrapper_open")) {
                $(".scope_open", $scopeWrapper).removeClass("scope_open");
                $scopeWrapper.removeClass("wrapper_open");
                //$(this).attr("value", $(this).attr("data-old-value"));
                $scopeSelBtnlabel.html($(this).attr("data-old-value"));
                $(this).removeAttr("data-old-value");
            } else {
                var $childSelected = $(".scope_has_child .scope_selector_submenu .scope_selector_selected", $scopeWrapper);
                $childSelected.parents(".scope_has_child")
                    .first().addClass("scope_open")
                    .children(".scope_selector_item ").addClass("scope_selector_selected");
                $(this).attr("data-old-value", $scopeSelBtnlabel.html());
                $scopeSelBtnlabel.html("Filtrer par");
                $scopeWrapper.addClass("wrapper_open");
                updateScopeSelectorPosition();
                $childSelected.parents(".scope_selector_submenu").scrollTop($childSelected.top);
            }
        });
        $(window).on('scroll resize', function () {
            if ($scopeWrapper.hasClass("wrapper_open")) {
                updateScopeSelectorPosition();
            }
        });
    });
      </script>

               $(document).ready(function () {

        // Fallback placeholder HTML5
        if (!Modernizr.input.placeholder)
            jQuery('#RechercheTextesNonCodifies').find("[placeholder]").placeholder();

        $("#RechercheTextesNonCodifies .empty-button").emptyButton();

        // Chargement de la conf pour le bloc "Textes non codifiés"
        var searchBlockConfig = new SearchBlock.SearchBlockConfig();
        $.ajax({
            url: GetRoot() + "RechercheJurisprudence/GetSearchBlockConfig",
            data: {
                htmlid: "source-tnc"
            },
            success: function (response) {
                searchBlockConfig.applySearchBlockConfig(response);
            }
        });

        var tnc = new SearchBlock.TextesNonCodifies({SourcesSpecificCodes : {"dateTranspoArea":"directive"}});
        tnc.initialize();
        tnc.setTNCUfd({ listWidthFixed: false });

    });

    $(document).ready(function () {

        try {
            if (!Modernizr.input.placeholder) $('[placeholder]').placeholder();
        } catch (e) {
            $('[placeholder]').placeholder();
        }

        $(".search-links span").live("click", function (e) {
            $('form').triggerHandler('submit');
            e.preventDefault();
            var keyword = $("#keyword").val() == "" ? "_empty" : $("#keyword").val();

            window.open('https://www.dalloz.fr/documentation/'+'Recherche?as=' + keyword, "_self");
        });

    });
   </script>
